(function () {
    var host = window.location.host.split('.').slice(0, -1).join('.');
    var uaEqGoogleMobile = /Mobile.*GoogleBot/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
    var redirect = function (current, target, hash) {
        if (window.location.hostname !== target) {
            window.redirectInPlace = true;
            window.location.href = window.location.href.replace(current, target).replace(".bild.html", ".bildMobile.html") + hash;
        }
    };
    var cookieSwitchName = [];
    var hash = '';
    window.redirectInPlace = false;
    if (window.location.hash.toLowerCase().indexOf('cvd') === -1 && ["www.preview.bildcms.de", "m.preview.bildcms.de"].indexOf(window.location.hostname) === -1 && ['m.bild', 'www.bild'].indexOf(host) > -1) {
        document.cookie = "mobileSwitch=wap; path=/; domain=.bild.de; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;";
        cookieSwitchName = document.cookie.split(";").map(function (cookieValue) {
            return cookieValue.split("=")[0].trim();
        });
        if (document.referrer) {
            hash = '###wt_ref=' + encodeURIComponent(document.referrer) + '&wt_t=' + Date.now();
        }
        if (cookieSwitchName.indexOf("noDesktop") > -1) {
            redirect("www.bild.de", "m.bild.de", hash);
        } else if (cookieSwitchName.indexOf("noMobile") > -1) {
            redirect("m.bild.de", "www.bild.de", hash);
        } else {
            if (window.matchMedia('(max-width: 767px)').matches && !uaEqGoogleMobile) {
                redirect("www.bild.de", "m.bild.de", hash);
            } else {
                redirect("m.bild.de", "www.bild.de", hash);
            }
        }
    }
})();</script>

            var remCallback = de.bild.tracking.rem ? de.bild.tracking.rem.remCallback : function(){};

            var rem = new Object();
            rem.shopid = { name:"shopid", value:"bdep"};
            rem.action = { name:"action", value:"pageview"};
            rem.origin = { name:"origin", value:"web"};
            rem.contentid = { name:"contentid", value:"Home/body/HOME"};
            rem.coremediaid = { name:"coremediaid", value:"16237890"};
            rem.doctype = { name:"doctype", value:"BTOSeite"};
            rem.adstate = { name:"adstate", value:"on/on/home///_index/"};
            rem.accesstype = { name:"accesstype", value:"free"};
            rem.visibility = { name:"visibility", value:"visible"};
            rem.channel = { name:"channel", value:"Home"};
            rem.subchannel = { name:"subchannel", value:"HOME"};
            rem.subsubchannel = { name:"subsubchannel", value:""};
            rem.heading = { name:"heading", value:""};
            rem.kicker = { name:"kicker", value:""};
            rem.kid = { name:"kid", value:""};
            rem.conversion = { name:"conversion", value:"false"};

            


            //es dürfen keine leeren Parameter an REM übergeben werden.
            function evaluate(remObj)
            {
                var remparams = new Array();

                for(var propertyName in remObj)
                {
                    if (remObj[propertyName].value)
                    {
                        remparams.push(remObj[propertyName]);
                    }
                }
                return remparams;
            }

            function triggerRemRequest() {
                if (typeof(rem_client) != "undefined")
                {
                    rem_client.request(evaluate(rem),['remCallback']);
                    
                    if(rem.conversion.value === "true"){
                        de.bild.utils.storage.set("contentid",rem.contentid.value,true);
                        de.bild.utils.storage.set("coremediaid",rem.coremediaid.value,true);
                    }
                }

            }
           </script>

        <script>
            (function (scriptSrc, callback) {
                var headTag = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
                var scriptTag = document.createElement('script');
                scriptTag.src = scriptSrc;
                scriptTag.async = true;
                scriptTag.onload = callback;
                scriptTag.onreadystatechange = function() {
                    if (this.readyState == 'complete') {
                        callback();
                    }
                }
                headTag.appendChild(scriptTag);
            })("https://rem-track.bild.de/rem-1.1/static/remclient/1.1/remclient_with_clicktracking.js ", triggerRemRequest);
        </script>

                    remEnd.accesstype = rem.accesstype;
                    remEnd.visibility = { name:"visibility", value:"visible"};
                    remEnd.conversion = { name:"conversion", value:"true"};

                    if (typeof(rem_client) != "undefined")                {
                        rem_client.request(evaluate(remEnd),['remCallback']);
                        de.bild.utils.storage.set("contentid", remEnd.contentid.value, true);
                        de.bild.utils.storage.set("coremediaid", remEnd.coremediaid.value, true);
                    }
                }
            
        }
    </script>
<script>
    </script>
</div>

			<header id="anker-46448292">
                <h2>
                    Alle Meldungen</h2>

	<div class="tlw-15 clearfix">

    <!-- Teaserreihe -->
    <div class="misc
                      posLast"  data-tr-teaser-home-31="bi=31|ti=4|id=46448290">
                <link rel="stylesheet" href="/code/seo-widget,46782346.7.bild.css"> <script> </script>

<div class="rssFeed_seo_widget">
    <div class="rssFeed_seo_widget_block1"></div>
    <div class="rssFeed_seo_widget_block2"></div>

<script>
// FUNKTIONIERT NUR PUBLIZIERT WEGEN COP
(function($){
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: "https://www.bild.de/rssfeeds/rss4/rss4-45554522,feed=feedreader-home-seo-widget.bild.html",
        dataType: "xml"
    }).done(function(xml) {
        var index = 1;
        $(xml).find('item').each(function() {
            var title = $(this).find('title').text();
            var link = $(this).find('link').text();
            var pubDate = $(this).find('pubDate').text();
            var startTime = new Date(pubDate);
            var endTime = new Date();
            var difference = endTime.getTime() - startTime.getTime(); // This will give difference in milliseconds
            var resultInMinutes = Math.round(difference / 60000);
            var result = "";
            if (startTime.getDate() === endTime.getDate() && startTime.getMonth() === endTime.getMonth()) {
                if (resultInMinutes > 60) {
                    var minutes = startTime.getMinutes();
                    if (minutes.toString().length === 1) {
                        minutes = "0" + minutes;
                    }
                    result = startTime.getHours() + ":" + minutes + " Uhr";
                }
                if (resultInMinutes <= 60) {
                    result = "Vor " + resultInMinutes + " Minuten";
                }
            } else {
                result = startTime.getDate() + "." + (startTime.getMonth() + 1) + "." + startTime.getFullYear();
            }
            if (index <= 9) {
                $(".rssFeed_seo_widget_block1").append("<span class='rssFeedItem" + index + "'><p class='pubDate'>" + result + "</p><p class='title'><a href='" + link + "' alt='" + title + "'>" + title + "</a></p></span>");
            } else {
                $(".rssFeed_seo_widget_block2").append("<span class='rssFeedItem" + index + "'><p class='pubDate'>" + result + "</p><p class='title'><a href='" + link + "' alt='" + title + "'>" + title + "</a></p></span>");
            }
            index++;
            if (index === 19) {
                return false;
            }
        });
    }).fail(function() {
        console.log('FAILED to Parse RSS... Try Again...');
    });
})(jQuery); </script>


</div>
